#define CPPHTTPLIB_OPENSSL_SUPPORT
#include "httplib.h"
#include "json.hpp"
#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
#include <queue>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <unordered_set>
#include <cmath>
#include <limits>
#include <algorithm>
#include <iomanip> // For currency formatting
using namespace std;

// Define route types
enum RouteType {
    FASTEST,
    SHORTEST,
    AVOID_TOLLS,
    SCENIC
};

// Toll information structure
struct TollInfo {
    string name;
    string operator_name;
    double cost;
    string currency;
    
    TollInfo(const string& n, const string& op, double c, const string& curr = "IDR")
        : name(n), operator_name(op), cost(c), currency(curr) {}
};

// Forward declarations
string extractCityName(const string& fullDisplayName);

// Structure to represent a location
struct Location {
    string name;
    double lat;
    double lon;
    
    Location(const string& n, double latitude, double longitude) 
        : name(n), lat(latitude), lon(longitude) {}
    
    Location() : lat(0), lon(0) {}
};

// Structure to represent a graph node
struct Node {
    string id;
    Location location;
    vector<pair<string, double>> edges; // adjacency list: (node_id, distance)
    
    // Constructor with parameters
    Node(const string& nodeId, const Location& loc) 
        : id(nodeId), location(loc) {}
    
    // Add a default constructor to fix the error
    Node() {}
};

// Helper function to extract city name from Nominatim response
string extractCityName(const string& fullDisplayName) {
    // Nominatim typically returns: "City, Region, Province, Country"
    // We want to extract just the city part
    size_t firstComma = fullDisplayName.find(',');
    if (firstComma != string::npos) {
        return fullDisplayName.substr(0, firstComma);
    }
    return fullDisplayName; // Return full name if no comma found
}

// Add accurate city distance data
unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, double>> getAccurateCityDistances() {
    unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, double>> distances;
    
    // Add accurate distances for major Indonesian cities (in km)
    distances["Surabaya"]["Gresik"] = 32.5;
    distances["Gresik"]["Surabaya"] = 32.5;
    
    distances["Surabaya"]["Sidoarjo"] = 25.0;
    distances["Sidoarjo"]["Surabaya"] = 25.0;
    
    distances["Surabaya"]["Malang"] = 95.0;
    distances["Malang"]["Surabaya"] = 95.0;
    
    distances["Surabaya"]["Mojokerto"] = 50.0;
    distances["Mojokerto"]["Surabaya"] = 50.0;
    
    distances["Surabaya"]["Lamongan"] = 47.0;
    distances["Lamongan"]["Surabaya"] = 47.0;
    
    distances["Jakarta"]["Bogor"] = 59.0;
    distances["Bogor"]["Jakarta"] = 59.0;
    
    distances["Jakarta"]["Bekasi"] = 28.0;
    distances["Bekasi"]["Jakarta"] = 28.0;
    
    distances["Jakarta"]["Tangerang"] = 25.0;
    distances["Tangerang"]["Jakarta"] = 25.0;
    
    distances["Jakarta"]["Bandung"] = 151.0;
    distances["Bandung"]["Jakarta"] = 151.0;
    
    distances["Yogyakarta"]["Solo"] = 65.0;
    distances["Solo"]["Yogyakarta"] = 65.0;
    
    distances["Yogyakarta"]["Semarang"] = 110.0;
    distances["Semarang"]["Yogyakarta"] = 110.0;
    
    distances["Bandung"]["Cimahi"] = 15.0;
    distances["Cimahi"]["Bandung"] = 15.0;
    
    return distances;
}

// Function to get routing details from OSRM with route type parameter
vector<string> getRouteDetails(const Location& start, const Location& end, RouteType routeType = FASTEST) {
    vector<string> steps;
    
    // Convert route type to OSRM parameters
    string routeParams;
    switch (routeType) {
        case FASTEST:
            routeParams = "steps=true&overview=full";
            break;
        case SHORTEST:
            routeParams = "steps=true&overview=full&alternatives=false&geometries=geojson";
            break;
        case AVOID_TOLLS:
            routeParams = "steps=true&overview=full&exclude=toll";
            break;
        case SCENIC:
            routeParams = "steps=true&overview=full";
            break;
        default:
            routeParams = "steps=true&overview=full";
    }
    
    // Format: https://router.project-osrm.org/route/v1/driving/start_lon,start_lat;end_lon,end_lat?steps=true
    string url = "router.project-osrm.org";
    string path = "/route/v1/driving/" + 
                  to_string(start.lon) + "," + to_string(start.lat) + ";" +
                  to_string(end.lon) + "," + to_string(end.lat) + 
                  "?" + routeParams;
    
    httplib::Client cli("https://" + url);
    httplib::Headers headers = {
        {"User-Agent", "MapsPathfinder/1.0"}
    };
    
    auto res = cli.Get(path.c_str(), headers);
    
    if (res && res->status == 200) {
        try {
            auto json = nlohmann::json::parse(res->body);
            auto& routes = json["routes"];
            
            if (!routes.empty()) {
                auto& legs = routes[0]["legs"];
                if (!legs.empty()) {
                    auto& steps_json = legs[0]["steps"];
                    for (auto& step : steps_json) {
                        // Extract the maneuver and road name
                        string maneuver = step["maneuver"]["type"];
                        string road_name = "unnamed road";
                        
                        if (step.contains("name") && !step["name"].is_null() && !step["name"].get<string>().empty()) {
                            road_name = step["name"];
                        }
                        
                        // Clean up the maneuver text
                        if (maneuver == "depart") maneuver = "Start";
                        else if (maneuver == "arrive") maneuver = "Arrive";
                        else if (maneuver == "turn") {
                            string modifier = step["maneuver"]["modifier"];
                            maneuver = "Turn " + modifier;
                        }
                        
                        // Only add meaningful steps (not too many "continue" steps)
                        if (maneuver != "continue" || steps.size() < 2) {
                            steps.push_back(road_name);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (const exception& e) {
            cerr << "Error parsing OSRM response: " << e.what() << endl;
        }
    }
    
    // If API fails or returns empty, use our fallback data
    if (steps.empty()) {
        // Enhanced map of known routes with more detailed areas
        static unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<string>>> detailedRoutes = {
            {"Surabaya", {
                {"Gresik", {"Jalan Margomulyo", "Jalan Tambak Osowilangun", "Jalan Gresik Gadukan", "Jalan Gresik"}},
                {"Sidoarjo", {"Jalan Ahmad Yani", "Jalan Jenggolo", "Jalan Waru", "Jalan Gedangan"}},
                {"Malang", {"Jalan A. Yani", "Jalan Waru", "Tol Sidoarjo-Porong", "Tol Porong-Pandaan", "Tol Pandaan-Malang", "Jalan Raya Malang"}},
                {"Mojokerto", {"Tol Surabaya-Mojokerto", "Jalan Bypass Krian", "Jalan Raya Mojosari", "Jalan Jayanegara"}},
                {"Lamongan", {"Jalan Raya Gresik", "Jalan Daendels", "Jalan Raya Lamongan"}}
            }},
            {"Jakarta", {
                {"Bogor", {"Jalan TB Simatupang", "Tol Jagorawi", "Jalan Pajajaran", "Jalan Raya Bogor"}},
                {"Bandung", {"Tol Jakarta-Cikampek", "Tol Cipularang", "Tol Padalarang-Cileunyi", "Jalan Pasteur"}},
                {"Bekasi", {"Tol Jakarta Timur", "Jalan Kalimalang", "Jalan Ahmad Yani Bekasi"}},
                {"Tangerang", {"Tol Jakarta-Tangerang", "Jalan Daan Mogot", "Jalan Sudirman Tangerang"}}
            }},
            {"Yogyakarta", {
                {"Solo", {"Jalan Solo", "Jalan Prambanan", "Jalan Klaten", "Jalan Slamet Riyadi"}},
                {"Semarang", {"Jalan Magelang", "Jalan Secang", "Jalan Raya Ambarawa", "Jalan Semarang"}},
                {"Magelang", {"Jalan Palagan", "Jalan Yogya-Magelang", "Jalan Pemuda Magelang"}}
            }},
            {"Bandung", {
                {"Cimahi", {"Jalan Sukajadi", "Jalan Pasteur", "Jalan Cimahi"}},
                {"Garut", {"Jalan Soekarno-Hatta", "Tol Cileunyi", "Jalan Raya Nagreg", "Jalan Raya Garut"}},
                {"Jakarta", {"Jalan Pasteur", "Tol Padalarang", "Tol Cipularang", "Tol Jakarta-Cikampek", "Jalan Gatot Subroto"}}
            }}
        };
        
        // Get the detailed route if available
        string startCity = extractCityName(start.name);
        string endCity = extractCityName(end.name);
        
        auto it1 = detailedRoutes.find(startCity);
        if (it1 != detailedRoutes.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(endCity);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                // For avoiding tolls, filter out toll roads
                if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
                    vector<string> noTollRoute;
                    for (const auto& road : it2->second) {
                        if (road.find("Tol") == string::npos) {
                            noTollRoute.push_back(road);
                        } else {
                            // Replace toll roads with alternative routes
                            if (road == "Tol Jakarta-Cikampek") {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Bekasi");
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Cikarang");
                            } else if (road == "Tol Cipularang") {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Puncak");
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Cianjur");
                            } else {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Alternatif (Non-Tol)");
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    return noTollRoute;
                }
                
                // For scenic routes, add some scenic paths
                if (routeType == SCENIC) {
                    vector<string> scenicRoute = it2->second;
                    if (startCity == "Jakarta" && endCity == "Bandung") {
                        scenicRoute = {"Jalan Puncak", "Taman Safari", "Jalur Pemandangan Gunung Gede", "Cianjur", "Jalan Pemandangan Lembang"};
                    } else if (startCity == "Yogyakarta" && endCity == "Solo") {
                        scenicRoute = {"Jalan Kaliurang", "Pemandangan Merapi", "Jalur Wisata Tawangmangu", "Jalan Karanganyar"};
                    }
                    return scenicRoute;
                }
                
                return it2->second;
            }
        }
        
        // Check reverse direction
        it1 = detailedRoutes.find(endCity);
        if (it1 != detailedRoutes.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(startCity);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                vector<string> reversedAreas = it2->second;
                reverse(reversedAreas.begin(), reversedAreas.end());
                
                // Apply same filters for avoiding tolls/scenic routes
                if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
                    vector<string> noTollRoute;
                    for (const auto& road : reversedAreas) {
                        if (road.find("Tol") == string::npos) {
                            noTollRoute.push_back(road);
                        } else {
                            // Replace with alternatives
                            if (road == "Tol Jakarta-Cikampek") {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Bekasi");
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Cikarang");
                            } else if (road == "Tol Cipularang") {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Puncak");
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Raya Cianjur");
                            } else {
                                noTollRoute.push_back("Jalan Alternatif (Non-Tol)");
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    return noTollRoute;
                }
                
                if (routeType == SCENIC) {
                    vector<string> scenicRoute = reversedAreas;
                    if (endCity == "Jakarta" && startCity == "Bandung") {
                        scenicRoute = {"Jalan Pemandangan Lembang", "Cianjur", "Jalur Pemandangan Gunung Gede", "Taman Safari", "Jalan Puncak"};
                    } else if (endCity == "Yogyakarta" && startCity == "Solo") {
                        scenicRoute = {"Jalan Karanganyar", "Jalur Wisata Tawangmangu", "Pemandangan Merapi", "Jalan Kaliurang"};
                    }
                    return scenicRoute;
                }
                
                return reversedAreas;
            }
        }
        
        // If still no detailed route, fall back to original data
        static unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<string>>> knownRoutes = {
            {"Surabaya", {
                {"Sidoarjo", {"Wonokromo", "Waru", "Gedangan"}},
                {"Malang", {"Wonokromo", "Porong", "Pandaan", "Lawang", "Singosari"}},
                {"Gresik", {"Tandes", "Benowo"}},
                {"Mojokerto", {"Sepanjang", "Krian", "Mojosari"}},
                {"Lamongan", {"Gresik", "Duduk Sampeyan", "Manyar"}}
            }},
            {"Jakarta", {
                {"Bogor", {"Depok", "Cibinong"}},
                {"Bekasi", {"Cakung", "Tambun"}},
                {"Tangerang", {"Kalideres", "Batu Ceper"}},
                {"Bandung", {"Cikampek", "Purwakarta", "Padalarang"}}
            }},
            {"Yogyakarta", {
                {"Solo", {"Klaten", "Prambanan"}},
                {"Semarang", {"Magelang", "Salatiga", "Ungaran"}},
                {"Magelang", {"Sleman", "Tempel"}}
            }},
            {"Bandung", {
                {"Cimahi", {"Cihampelas", "Lembang"}},
                {"Garut", {"Nagreg", "Leles", "Kadungora"}},
                {"Jakarta", {"Padalarang", "Purwakarta", "Cikampek", "Bekasi"}}
            }}
        };
        
        // Modify routes based on route type
        if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
            // Non-toll alternatives
            knownRoutes["Jakarta"]["Bandung"] = {"Puncak", "Cianjur", "Padalarang"};
            knownRoutes["Surabaya"]["Malang"] = {"Wonokromo", "Gempol", "Bangil", "Lawang", "Singosari"};
        } else if (routeType == SCENIC) {
            // Scenic alternatives
            knownRoutes["Jakarta"]["Bandung"] = {"Puncak", "Cianjur", "Lembang"};
            knownRoutes["Yogyakarta"]["Solo"] = {"Kaliurang", "Tawangmangu", "Karanganyar"};
        }
        
        // Convert to lowercase for case-insensitive comparison
        auto toLower = [](string s) {
            transform(s.begin(), s.end(), s.begin(), [](unsigned char c) { return tolower(c); });
            return s;
        };
        
        string startLower = toLower(startCity);
        string endLower = toLower(endCity);
        
        // Check all known routes (both directions)
        for (const auto& cityRoutesPair : knownRoutes) {
            string city1 = cityRoutesPair.first;
            const auto& routes = cityRoutesPair.second;
            
            if (toLower(city1) == startLower) {
                for (const auto& cityAreasPair : routes) {
                    string city2 = cityAreasPair.first;
                    const auto& areas = cityAreasPair.second;
                    
                    if (toLower(city2) == endLower) {
                        return areas; // Found a route
                    }
                }
            }
            // Check reverse direction
            if (toLower(city1) == endLower) {
                for (const auto& cityAreasPair : routes) {
                    string city2 = cityAreasPair.first;
                    const auto& areas = cityAreasPair.second;
                    
                    if (toLower(city2) == startLower) {
                        // Return the areas in reverse order
                        vector<string> reversedAreas = areas;
                        reverse(reversedAreas.begin(), reversedAreas.end());
                        return reversedAreas;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    return steps;
}

// Calculate distance between two coordinates using Haversine formula (in kilometers)
double calculateDistance(double lat1, double lon1, double lat2, double lon2) {
    const double R = 6371.0; // Earth radius in kilometers
    double dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * M_PI / 180.0;
    double dLon = (lon2 - lon1) * M_PI / 180.0;
    
    double a = sin(dLat/2) * sin(dLat/2) +
               cos(lat1 * M_PI / 180.0) * cos(lat2 * M_PI / 180.0) *
               sin(dLon/2) * sin(dLon/2);
    double c = 2 * atan2(sqrt(a), sqrt(1-a));
    return R * c;
}

// Update the distance calculation to use accurate city distances when available
double getAccurateDistance(const Location& start, const Location& end) {
    static auto cityDistances = getAccurateCityDistances();
    
    string startCity = extractCityName(start.name);
    string endCity = extractCityName(end.name);
    
    // Try to find a known distance
    auto it1 = cityDistances.find(startCity);
    if (it1 != cityDistances.end()) {
        auto it2 = it1->second.find(endCity);
        if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
            return it2->second;  // Return the known accurate distance
        }
    }
    
    // Fall back to Haversine formula if no known distance
    return calculateDistance(start.lat, start.lon, end.lat, end.lon);
}

// Get toll information for a route
vector<TollInfo> getTollInfo(const Location& start, const Location& end, RouteType routeType, 
                          double& totalCost, string& currency) {
    vector<TollInfo> tolls;
    totalCost = 0;
    currency = "IDR"; // Default to Indonesian Rupiah
    
    // Skip toll calculation if we're avoiding tolls
    if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
        return tolls;
    }
    
    // In a real app, this would make an API call to TollGuru
    // For now, use hardcoded data for known routes
    string startCity = extractCityName(start.name);
    string endCity = extractCityName(end.name);
    
    // Database of toll information for common routes
    static unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<TollInfo>>> knownTolls = {
        {"Jakarta", {
            {"Bogor", {
                TollInfo("Jagorawi Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 15000),
                TollInfo("Jakarta Inner Ring Road", "Jasa Marga", 10000)
            }},
            {"Bandung", {
                TollInfo("Cipularang Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 35000),
                TollInfo("Jakarta-Cikampek Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 25000)
            }},
            {"Bekasi", {
                TollInfo("Jakarta-Cikampek Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 12000)
            }},
            {"Tangerang", {
                TollInfo("Jakarta-Tangerang Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 11000)
            }}
        }},
        {"Surabaya", {
            {"Sidoarjo", {
                TollInfo("Surabaya-Gempol Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 7500)
            }},
            {"Malang", {
                TollInfo("Surabaya-Malang Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 28000)
            }},
            {"Gresik", {
                TollInfo("MERR Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 7000)
            }},
            {"Mojokerto", {
                TollInfo("Surabaya-Mojokerto Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 17500)
            }}
        }},
        {"Bandung", {
            {"Jakarta", {
                TollInfo("Cipularang Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 35000),
                TollInfo("Jakarta-Cikampek Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 25000)
            }},
            {"Cimahi", {
                TollInfo("Padalarang-Cileunyi Toll Road", "Jasa Marga", 8000)
            }}
        }}
    };
    
    // Try to find toll data for this route
    auto it1 = knownTolls.find(startCity);
    if (it1 != knownTolls.end()) {
        auto it2 = it1->second.find(endCity);
        if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
            tolls = it2->second;
            for (const auto& toll : tolls) {
                totalCost += toll.cost;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Try reverse direction
    if (tolls.empty()) {
        it1 = knownTolls.find(endCity);
        if (it1 != knownTolls.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(startCity);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                tolls = it2->second;
                for (const auto& toll : tolls) {
                    totalCost += toll.cost;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // If tolls is still empty, check if distance is significant and add a generic toll
    if (tolls.empty() && getAccurateDistance(start, end) > 50) {
        double distance = getAccurateDistance(start, end);
        // Estimate toll cost at IDR 1000 per km (for major highways in Indonesia)
        double estimatedCost = distance * 1000;
        tolls.push_back(TollInfo("Estimated Toll", "Various Operators", estimatedCost));
        totalCost = estimatedCost;
    }
    
    return tolls;
}

// Format currency values properly
string formatCurrency(double amount, const string& currency) {
    stringstream ss;
    ss << fixed << setprecision(0); // No decimal for IDR
    
    if (currency == "IDR") {
        ss << "Rp " << amount;
    } else if (currency == "USD") {
        ss << "$" << amount;
    } else if (currency == "EUR") {
        ss << "€" << amount;
    } else {
        ss << amount << " " << currency;
    }
    
    return ss.str();
}

// Geocode a location name to coordinates using Nominatim API
Location geocodeLocation(const string& locationName) {
    httplib::Client cli("https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org");
    
    httplib::Headers headers = {
        {"User-Agent", "MapsPathfinder/1.0"}
    };
    
    auto res = cli.Get("/search?q=" + httplib::detail::encode_url(locationName) + 
                       "&format=json&limit=1", headers);
    
    if (res && res->status == 200) {
        try {
            auto json = nlohmann::json::parse(res->body);
            if (!json.empty()) {
                double lat = stod(json[0]["lat"].get<string>());
                double lon = stod(json[0]["lon"].get<string>());
                
                // Extract just the city name from the full display_name
                string fullName = json[0]["display_name"].get<string>();
                string cityName = extractCityName(fullName);
                
                return Location(cityName, lat, lon);
            }
        } catch (const exception& e) {
            cerr << "Error parsing JSON: " << e.what() << endl;
        }
    }
    
    return Location(); // Return empty location if geocoding failed
}

// Greedy Best-First Search algorithm for finding routes
vector<string> findBestFirstPath(
    const unordered_map<string, Node>& graph,
    const string& startId,
    const string& endId) {
    
    // Priority queue using only heuristic (not f_score like A*)
    priority_queue<pair<double, string>, 
                  vector<pair<double, string>>,
                  greater<pair<double, string>>> openSet;
    
    unordered_map<string, string> cameFrom;
    unordered_set<string> closedSet;
    
    // Initialize with start node
    openSet.push(make_pair(
        getAccurateDistance(
            graph.at(startId).location,
            graph.at(endId).location
        ), 
        startId
    ));
    
    while (!openSet.empty()) {
        string current = openSet.top().second;
        openSet.pop();
        
        // If we reached the goal
        if (current == endId) {
            // Reconstruct path
            vector<string> path;
            while (current != startId) {
                path.push_back(current);
                current = cameFrom[current];
            }
            path.push_back(startId);
            reverse(path.begin(), path.end());
            return path;
        }
        
        // Add current to closed set
        closedSet.insert(current);
        
        // Check all neighbors
        for (const auto& neighbor : graph.at(current).edges) {
            string neighborId = neighbor.first;
            
            // Skip if already evaluated
            if (closedSet.count(neighborId) > 0) {
                continue;
            }
            
            // Calculate heuristic (straight-line distance to goal)
            double heuristic = getAccurateDistance(
                graph.at(neighborId).location,
                graph.at(endId).location
            );
            
            // If not in open set or better path found
            if (cameFrom.find(neighborId) == cameFrom.end()) {
                cameFrom[neighborId] = current;
                openSet.push(make_pair(heuristic, neighborId));
            }
        }
    }
    
    // No path found
    return {};
}

// Find shortest path using A* algorithm
vector<string> findShortestPath(
    const unordered_map<string, Node>& graph,
    const string& startId,
    const string& endId) {
    
    // Priority queue for A* algorithm
    // pair: (f_score, node_id) where f_score = g_score + heuristic
    priority_queue<pair<double, string>, 
                        vector<pair<double, string>>,
                        greater<pair<double, string>>> openSet;
    
    // Track visited nodes and parent relationships
    unordered_map<string, double> gScore;
    unordered_map<string, string> cameFrom;
    
    // Initialize
    for (const auto& node : graph) {
        gScore[node.first] = numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
    }
    
    gScore[startId] = 0;
    openSet.push(make_pair(
        getAccurateDistance(
            graph.at(startId).location,
            graph.at(endId).location
        ), 
        startId
    ));
    
    // A* algorithm
    while (!openSet.empty()) {
        string current = openSet.top().second;
        openSet.pop();
        
        if (current == endId) {
            // Reconstruct path
            vector<string> path;
            while (current != startId) {
                path.push_back(current);
                current = cameFrom[current];
            }
            path.push_back(startId);
            reverse(path.begin(), path.end());
            return path;
        }
        
        for (const auto& neighbor : graph.at(current).edges) {
            string neighborId = neighbor.first;
            double distance = neighbor.second;
            
            double tentativeGScore = gScore[current] + distance;
            
            if (tentativeGScore < gScore[neighborId]) {
                cameFrom[neighborId] = current;
                gScore[neighborId] = tentativeGScore;
                
                double heuristic = getAccurateDistance(
                    graph.at(neighborId).location,
                    graph.at(endId).location
                );
                
                double fScore = tentativeGScore + heuristic;
                openSet.push(make_pair(fScore, neighborId));
            }
        }
    }
    
    // No path found
    return {};
}

// Generate alternate routes with improved waypoints
vector<vector<string>> generateMultipleRoutes(
    unordered_map<string, Node>& graph,
    const string& startId,
    const string& endId,
    const Location& startLocation,
    const Location& endLocation,
    RouteType routeType = FASTEST) {
    
    vector<vector<string>> routes;
    
    // Add the direct route using Best-First Search (greedy approach)
    vector<string> directPath = findBestFirstPath(graph, startId, endId);
    if (!directPath.empty()) {
        routes.push_back(directPath);
    }
    
    // Create intermediate locations for alternative routes
    vector<Location> intermediateLocations;
    
    // Known intermediate cities for common routes (more realistic alternatives)
    string startCity = extractCityName(startLocation.name);
    string endCity = extractCityName(endLocation.name);
    
    static unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<string>>> knownIntermediates = {
        {"Surabaya", {
            {"Gresik", {"Tandes", "Benowo"}}, 
            {"Sidoarjo", {"Wonokromo", "Waru"}},
            {"Malang", {"Sidoarjo", "Pandaan", "Lawang"}}
        }},
        {"Jakarta", {
            {"Bandung", {"Bekasi", "Purwakarta", "Cimahi"}},
            {"Bogor", {"Depok", "Cibinong"}}
        }}
    };
    
    // Try to find known intermediate cities
    bool foundKnownRoute = false;
    auto it1 = knownIntermediates.find(startCity);
    if (it1 != knownIntermediates.end()) {
        auto it2 = it1->second.find(endCity);
        if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
            foundKnownRoute = true;
            const auto& waypoints = it2->second;
            
            // Add these known waypoints
            for (size_t i = 0; i < waypoints.size(); i++) {
                string nodeId = "known_waypoint" + to_string(i+1);
                
                // Create a location that's geographically sensible
                double ratio = (i+1.0) / (waypoints.size()+1.0);
                double lat = startLocation.lat + (endLocation.lat - startLocation.lat) * ratio;
                double lon = startLocation.lon + (endLocation.lon - startLocation.lon) * ratio;
                
                Location wp(waypoints[i], lat, lon);
                graph[nodeId] = Node(nodeId, wp);
                
                // Connect waypoints in sequence
                if (i == 0) {
                    // Connect start to first waypoint
                    double dist = getAccurateDistance(startLocation, wp);
                    graph[startId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, dist));
                    
                    // Connect first waypoint to end
                    dist = getAccurateDistance(wp, endLocation);
                    graph[nodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, dist));
                } else {
                    // Connect previous waypoint to this one
                    string prevId = "known_waypoint" + to_string(i);
                    double dist = getAccurateDistance(graph[prevId].location, wp);
                    graph[prevId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, dist));
                    
                    // Connect this waypoint to end
                    dist = getAccurateDistance(wp, endLocation);
                    graph[nodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, dist));
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // If no known route, create reasonable waypoints
    if (!foundKnownRoute) {
        // For AVOID_TOLLS and SCENIC routes, we'll generate more alternative paths
        if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS || routeType == SCENIC) {
            // Create some intermediate locations to generate alternate routes
            vector<Location> intermediateLocations;
            
            // Generate some intermediate points
            double lat_diff = endLocation.lat - startLocation.lat;
            double lon_diff = endLocation.lon - startLocation.lon;
            
            // Add intermediate locations slightly off the direct path
            for (int i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
                // Calculate position (25%, 50%, 75% of the way)
                double ratio = i / 4.0;
                
                // Add some randomness for alternate routes
                double latOffset = (i % 2 == 0) ? 0.01 : -0.01;
                double lonOffset = (i % 2 == 0) ? -0.01 : 0.01;
                
                // For scenic routes, add more deviation
                if (routeType == SCENIC) {
                    latOffset *= 2;
                    lonOffset *= 2;
                }
                
                // Create the intermediate location with a clear name
                string pointName = extractCityName(startLocation.name) + " to " + 
                                  extractCityName(endLocation.name) + 
                                  " (via Point " + to_string(i) + ")";
                
                Location intermediate(
                    pointName,
                    startLocation.lat + lat_diff * ratio + latOffset,
                    startLocation.lon + lon_diff * ratio + lonOffset
                );
                intermediateLocations.push_back(intermediate);
                
                // Add to graph
                string nodeId = "waypoint" + to_string(i);
                graph[nodeId] = Node(nodeId, intermediate);
            }
            
            // Connect the nodes to create alternate routes
            for (size_t i = 0; i < intermediateLocations.size(); i++) {
                string nodeId = "waypoint" + to_string(i+1);
                
                // Connect start to waypoint
                graph[startId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, 
                    getAccurateDistance(
                        graph[startId].location, 
                        graph[nodeId].location
                    )
                ));
                
                // Connect waypoint to end
                graph[nodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, 
                    getAccurateDistance(
                        graph[nodeId].location, 
                        graph[endId].location
                    )
                ));
                
                // Connect waypoints to each other for more route options
                if (i > 0) {
                    string prevNodeId = "waypoint" + to_string(i);
                    graph[prevNodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, 
                        getAccurateDistance(
                            graph[prevNodeId].location, 
                            graph[nodeId].location
                        )
                    ));
                }
            }
        } else {
            // Create some artificial waypoints that don't stray too far from reasonable paths
            for (int i = 1; i <= 2; i++) {
                double ratio = i / 3.0;
                
                // Much smaller offset for more reasonable routes
                double latOffset = (i % 2 == 0) ? 0.005 : -0.005;
                double lonOffset = (i % 2 == 0) ? -0.005 : 0.005;
                
                string pointName = extractCityName(startLocation.name) + " to " + 
                                  extractCityName(endLocation.name) + 
                                  " (via Point " + to_string(i) + ")";
                
                Location intermediate(
                    pointName,
                    startLocation.lat + (endLocation.lat - startLocation.lat) * ratio + latOffset,
                    startLocation.lon + (endLocation.lon - startLocation.lon) * ratio + lonOffset
                );
                
                string nodeId = "waypoint" + to_string(i);
                graph[nodeId] = Node(nodeId, intermediate);
                
                // Connect in a more sensible way
                if (i == 1) {
                    double dist = getAccurateDistance(startLocation, intermediate);
                    graph[startId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, dist));
                    
                    dist = getAccurateDistance(intermediate, endLocation);
                    graph[nodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, dist));
                } else {
                    string prevId = "waypoint" + to_string(i-1);
                    double dist = getAccurateDistance(startLocation, intermediate);
                    graph[startId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, dist));
                    
                    dist = getAccurateDistance(graph[prevId].location, intermediate);
                    graph[prevId].edges.push_back(make_pair(nodeId, dist));
                    
                    dist = getAccurateDistance(intermediate, endLocation);
                    graph[nodeId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, dist));
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Calculate alternate paths using both Best-First Search and A*
    vector<string> altPath1 = findBestFirstPath(graph, startId, endId);
    if (!altPath1.empty() && (routes.empty() || altPath1 != routes[0])) {
        routes.push_back(altPath1);
    }
    
    vector<string> altPath2 = findShortestPath(graph, startId, endId);
    if (!altPath2.empty() && (routes.empty() || altPath2 != routes[0]) && 
        (routes.size() < 2 || altPath2 != routes[1])) {
        routes.push_back(altPath2);
    }
    
    return routes;
}

// Function to format route as step-by-step directions with detailed areas from OSRM
string formatRouteWithRealDirections(
    const vector<string>& path,
    const unordered_map<string, Node>& graph,
    RouteType routeType = FASTEST) {
    
    if (path.empty()) return "No route available";
    
    string result;
    double totalDistance = 0;
    double totalTime = 0; // in minutes
    
    // Get toll information only for non-AVOID_TOLLS routes
    double tollCost = 0;
    string currency = "IDR";
    vector<TollInfo> tolls;
    
    // Only for direct routes (start to end)
    if (path.size() == 2 && path[0] == "start" && path[1] == "end") {
        const auto& startNode = graph.at(path[0]);
        const auto& endNode = graph.at(path[1]);
        
        // Get route details from OSRM
        vector<string> routeSteps = getRouteDetails(startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType);
        
        // Start with the city name
        result = extractCityName(startNode.location.name);
        
        // Add intermediate steps
        for (const auto& step : routeSteps) {
            result += " → " + step;
        }
        
        // End with destination city
        result += " → " + extractCityName(endNode.location.name);
        
        // Calculate distance using accurate distance
        totalDistance = getAccurateDistance(startNode.location, endNode.location);
        
        // Get toll information if not avoiding tolls
        if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS) {
            tolls = getTollInfo(startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType, tollCost, currency);
        }
    } else {
        // For routes with waypoints, use the original format
        for (size_t i = 0; i < path.size() - 1; i++) {
            const auto& currentNode = graph.at(path[i]);
            const auto& nextNode = graph.at(path[i+1]);
            
            // Find the edge to the next node
            double segmentDistance = 0;
            for (const auto& edge : currentNode.edges) {
                if (edge.first == path[i+1]) {
                    segmentDistance = edge.second;
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            result += currentNode.location.name;
            result += " → ";
            
            if (i == path.size() - 2) {
                result += nextNode.location.name;
            }
            
            totalDistance += segmentDistance;
        }
        
        // Get toll information for routes with waypoints
        if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS && path.size() >= 2) {
            const auto& startNode = graph.at(path.front());
            const auto& endNode = graph.at(path.back());
            tolls = getTollInfo(startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType, tollCost, currency);
        }
    }
    
    // Calculate estimated time (average 60 km/h)
    double speed = 60.0; // km/h
    switch (routeType) {
        case FASTEST: speed = 60.0; break;
        case SHORTEST: speed = 50.0; break; // Shorter but slower roads
        case AVOID_TOLLS: speed = 45.0; break; // Non-toll roads are slower
        case SCENIC: speed = 40.0; break; // Scenic routes are slower
    }
    totalTime = (totalDistance / speed) * 60; // Convert to minutes
    
    // Format result with distance and time
    int hours = static_cast<int>(totalTime) / 60;
    int minutes = static_cast<int>(totalTime) % 60;
    
    result += " (" + to_string(static_cast<int>(totalDistance)) + " km, ";
    if (hours > 0) {
        result += to_string(hours) + " hr ";
    }
    result += to_string(minutes) + " min)";
    
    // Add toll information if applicable
    if (!tolls.empty()) {
        result += "\nTotal Toll Cost: " + formatCurrency(tollCost, currency);
        result += "\nToll Details:";
        for (const auto& toll : tolls) {
            result += "\n  - " + toll.name + " (" + toll.operator_name + "): " + 
                     formatCurrency(toll.cost, toll.currency);
        }
    } else if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS) {
        result += "\nNo toll information available for this route.";
    } else {
        result += "\nThis route avoids all toll roads.";
    }
    
    return result;
}

// Regular format route function (without detailed areas)
string formatRoute(
    const vector<string>& path,
    const unordered_map<string, Node>& graph,
    RouteType routeType = FASTEST) {
    
    if (path.empty()) return "No route available";
    
    string result;
    double totalDistance = 0;
    double totalTime = 0; // in minutes
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < path.size() - 1; i++) {
        const auto& currentNode = graph.at(path[i]);
        const auto& nextNode = graph.at(path[i+1]);
        
        // Find the edge to the next node
        double segmentDistance = 0;
        for (const auto& edge : currentNode.edges) {
            if (edge.first == path[i+1]) {
                segmentDistance = edge.second;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        result += currentNode.location.name;
        result += " → ";
        
        if (i == path.size() - 2) {
            result += nextNode.location.name;
        }
        
        totalDistance += segmentDistance;
    }
    
    // Calculate estimated time (average speed depends on route type)
    double speed = 60.0; // km/h
    switch (routeType) {
        case FASTEST: speed = 60.0; break;
        case SHORTEST: speed = 50.0; break; // Shorter but slower roads
        case AVOID_TOLLS: speed = 45.0; break; // Non-toll roads are slower
        case SCENIC: speed = 40.0; break; // Scenic routes are slower
    }
    totalTime = (totalDistance / speed) * 60; // Convert to minutes
    
    // Format result with distance and time
    int hours = static_cast<int>(totalTime) / 60;
    int minutes = static_cast<int>(totalTime) % 60;
    
    result += " (" + to_string(static_cast<int>(totalDistance)) + " km, ";
    if (hours > 0) {
        result += to_string(hours) + " hr ";
    }
    result += to_string(minutes) + " min)";
    
    // Get toll information if not avoiding tolls
    if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS && path.size() >= 2) {
        double tollCost = 0;
        string currency = "IDR";
        const auto& startNode = graph.at(path.front());
        const auto& endNode = graph.at(path.back());
        vector<TollInfo> tolls = getTollInfo(startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType, tollCost, currency);
        
        if (!tolls.empty()) {
            result += "\nTotal Toll Cost: " + formatCurrency(tollCost, currency);
        }
    } else if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
        result += "\nThis route avoids all toll roads.";
    }
    
    return result;
}

// Main application
int main() {
    cout << "===== Maps Pathfinder Application =====" << endl;
    
    // Get start and end locations
    string startLocationName, endLocationName;
    
    cout << "Enter your current location: ";
    getline(cin, startLocationName);
    
    cout << "Enter your destination: ";
    getline(cin, endLocationName);
    
    cout << "\nSearching for locations..." << endl;
    
    // Geocode the locations
    Location startLocation = geocodeLocation(startLocationName);
    Location endLocation = geocodeLocation(endLocationName);
    
    if (startLocation.name.empty() || endLocation.name.empty()) {
        cerr << "Error: Could not find one or both locations." << endl;
        return 1;
    }
    
    cout << "Start: " << startLocation.name << endl;
    cout << "End: " << endLocation.name << endl;
    
    // Calculate direct distance using accurate distance
    double directDistance = getAccurateDistance(startLocation, endLocation);
    
    cout << "\nDirect distance: " << directDistance << " km" << endl;
    
    // Menu for route options
    bool exit = false;
    while (!exit) {
        cout << "\n===== Route Options =====" << endl;
        cout << "1. Fastest Route (Default)" << endl;
        cout << "2. Shortest Route" << endl;
        cout << "3. Avoid Tolls" << endl;
        cout << "4. Scenic Route" << endl;
        cout << "0. Exit" << endl;
        
        cout << "\nSelect an option: ";
        int choice;
        cin >> choice;
        cin.ignore(numeric_limits<streamsize>::max(), '\n'); // Clear input buffer
        
        RouteType routeType;
        
        switch (choice) {
            case 1:
                routeType = FASTEST;
                cout << "\nCalculating fastest route..." << endl;
                break;
            case 2:
                routeType = SHORTEST;
                cout << "\nCalculating shortest route..." << endl;
                break;
            case 3:
                routeType = AVOID_TOLLS;
                cout << "\nCalculating route avoiding tolls..." << endl;
                break;
            case 4:
                routeType = SCENIC;
                cout << "\nCalculating scenic route..." << endl;
                break;
            case 0:
                exit = true;
                cout << "Exiting program. Thank you for using Maps Pathfinder!" << endl;
                continue;
            default:
                cout << "Invalid option. Using Fastest Route." << endl;
                routeType = FASTEST;
                break;
        }
        
        if (!exit) {
            // For a real application, you would fetch the road network from an API
            // Here, we'll create a simple demo graph
            unordered_map<string, Node> graph;
            
            // In a real app, you would fetch the road network from an API like OSRM or GraphHopper
            // For this demo, we'll just use the direct path
            string startId = "start";
            string endId = "end";
            
            graph[startId] = Node(startId, startLocation);
            graph[endId] = Node(endId, endLocation);
            
            // Connect start and end directly (in a real app, this would be a road network)
            graph[startId].edges.push_back(make_pair(endId, directDistance));
            
            // Generate multiple routes
            vector<vector<string>> routes = generateMultipleRoutes(
                graph, startId, endId, startLocation, endLocation, routeType);
            
            if (routes.empty()) {
                cout << "No routes found between the locations." << endl;
                continue;
            }
            
            // Display routes with cleaner city names
            cout << "\n===== Available Routes between " 
                << extractCityName(startLocation.name) << " and " 
                << extractCityName(endLocation.name) << " =====" << endl;
            
            for (size_t i = 0; i < routes.size(); i++) {
                const auto& route = routes[i];
                cout << "Route " << (i+1) << ": ";
                
                if (i == 0) {
                    cout << "Recommended Route" << endl;
                } else {
                    cout << "Alternative Route " << i << endl;
                }
                
                // Use the real directions for the first (direct) route
                if (i == 0 && route.size() == 2) { // Direct route from start to end
                    cout << formatRouteWithRealDirections(route, graph, routeType) << endl;
                } else {
                    cout << formatRoute(route, graph, routeType) << endl;
                }
                
                // Show detailed step-by-step for each route
                cout << "Step-by-step directions:" << endl;
                
                if (i == 0 && route.size() == 2) { // Direct route from start to end
                    const auto& startNode = graph[route[0]];
                    const auto& endNode = graph[route[1]];
                    
                    // Get route details from OSRM
                    vector<string> routeSteps = getRouteDetails(startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType);
                    
                    // Calculate accurate distance
                    double totalDistance = getAccurateDistance(startNode.location, endNode.location);
                    
                    // Show start
                    cout << "  1. " << extractCityName(startNode.location.name);
                    
                    // Show intermediate steps
                    int stepNum = 2;
                    for (const auto& step : routeSteps) {
                        cout << " → " << step;
                    }
                    
                    // Show end and distance
                    cout << " → " << extractCityName(endNode.location.name);
                    
                    // Calculate time based on route type
                    double speed = 60.0;
                    switch (routeType) {
                        case FASTEST: speed = 60.0; break;
                        case SHORTEST: speed = 50.0; break;
                        case AVOID_TOLLS: speed = 45.0; break;
                        case SCENIC: speed = 40.0; break;
                    }
                    
                    double time = (totalDistance / speed) * 60; // minutes
                    int hours = static_cast<int>(time) / 60;
                    int minutes = static_cast<int>(time) % 60;
                    
                    cout << " (" << static_cast<int>(totalDistance) << " km, ";
                    if (hours > 0) {
                        cout << hours << " hr ";
                    }
                    cout << minutes << " min)" << endl;
                    
                    // Show toll information
                    if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS) {
                        double tollCost = 0;
                        string currency = "IDR";
                        vector<TollInfo> tolls = getTollInfo(
                            startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType, tollCost, currency);
                        
                        if (!tolls.empty()) {
                            cout << "  Toll Cost: " << formatCurrency(tollCost, currency) << endl;
                            for (const auto& toll : tolls) {
                                cout << "    - " << toll.name << ": " 
                                     << formatCurrency(toll.cost, toll.currency) << endl;
                            }
                        } else {
                            cout << "  No toll information available for this route." << endl;
                        }
                    } else {
                        cout << "  This route avoids all toll roads." << endl;
                    }
                    
                } else {
                    // For routes with waypoints, use the original step-by-step format
                    for (size_t j = 0; j < route.size() - 1; j++) {
                        const auto& currentNode = graph[route[j]];
                        const auto& nextNode = graph[route[j+1]];
                        
                        // Find the edge to the next node
                        double segmentDistance = 0;
                        for (const auto& edge : currentNode.edges) {
                            if (edge.first == route[j+1]) {
                                segmentDistance = edge.second;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // Calculate time based on route type
                        double speed = 60.0;
                        switch (routeType) {
                            case FASTEST: speed = 60.0; break;
                            case SHORTEST: speed = 50.0; break;
                            case AVOID_TOLLS: speed = 45.0; break;
                            case SCENIC: speed = 40.0; break;
                        }
                        
                        double time = (segmentDistance / speed) * 60; // minutes
                        
                        cout << "  " << (j+1) << ". " << currentNode.location.name 
                              << " → " << nextNode.location.name 
                              << " (" << static_cast<int>(segmentDistance) << " km, "
                              << static_cast<int>(time) << " min)" << endl;
                    }
                    
                    // Show toll information for the entire route
                    if (routeType != AVOID_TOLLS && route.size() >= 2) {
                        double tollCost = 0;
                        string currency = "IDR";
                        const auto& startNode = graph[route.front()];
                        const auto& endNode = graph[route.back()];
                        vector<TollInfo> tolls = getTollInfo(
                            startNode.location, endNode.location, routeType, tollCost, currency);
                        
                        if (!tolls.empty()) {
                            cout << "  Toll Cost: " << formatCurrency(tollCost, currency) << endl;
                            for (const auto& toll : tolls) {
                                cout << "    - " << toll.name << ": " 
                                     << formatCurrency(toll.cost, toll.currency) << endl;
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
                        cout << "  This route avoids all toll roads." << endl;
                    }
                }
                
                cout << endl;
            }
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}



## Update kode bawah##



#define CPPHTTPLIB_OPENSSL_SUPPORT
#include "httplib.h"
#include "json.hpp"
#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
#include <queue>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <unordered_set>
#include <cmath>
#include <limits>
#include <algorithm>
#include <iomanip> // For currency formatting
#include <stdexcept>
using namespace std;

// Define route types
enum RouteType {
    FASTEST,
    SHORTEST,
    AVOID_TOLLS,
    SCENIC
};

// Toll information structure
struct TollInfo {
    string name;
    string operator_name;
    double cost;
    string currency;
    
    TollInfo(const string& n, const string& op, double c, const string& curr = "IDR")
        : name(n), operator_name(op), cost(c), currency(curr) {}
};

// Forward declarations
string extractCityName(const string& fullDisplayName);

// Structure to represent a location
struct Location {
    string name;
    double lat;
    double lon;
    
    Location(const string& n, double latitude, double longitude) 
        : name(n), lat(latitude), lon(longitude) {}
    
    Location() : lat(0), lon(0) {}
};

// Structure to represent a graph node
struct Node {
    string id;
    Location location;
    vector<pair<string, double>> edges; // adjacency list: (node_id, distance)
    
    // Constructor with parameters
    Node(const string& nodeId, const Location& loc) 
        : id(nodeId), location(loc) {}
    
    // Add a default constructor to fix the error
    Node() {}
};

// Function to clean route symbols (replace unicode artifacts with proper arrows)
// Function to clean route symbols (replace unicode artifacts with proper arrows)
// Function to clean route symbols and convert all arrows to ASCII
string cleanRouteSymbols(const string& routeText) {
    string cleanedText = routeText;
    
    // Define all possible problematic symbols
    const vector<string> arrowSymbols = {"ΓåÆ", "Γå†", "→"};
    const string asciiArrow = " -> "; // Use ASCII arrow that works everywhere
    
    // Replace all arrow types with ASCII arrow
    for (const string& symbol : arrowSymbols) {
        size_t pos = 0;
        while((pos = cleanedText.find(symbol, pos)) != string::npos) {
            cleanedText.replace(pos, symbol.length(), asciiArrow);
            pos += asciiArrow.length();
        }
    }
    
    return cleanedText;
}

// Helper function to extract city name from Nominatim response
string extractCityName(const string& fullDisplayName) {
    // Nominatim typically returns: "City, Region, Province, Country"
    // We want to extract just the city part
    size_t firstComma = fullDisplayName.find(',');
    if (firstComma != string::npos) {
        return fullDisplayName.substr(0, firstComma);
    }
    return fullDisplayName; // Return full name if no comma found
}

// Enhanced Waypoint Database for better naming
struct WaypointDatabase {
    // Maps start city -> end city -> list of waypoint areas in order
    unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<string>>> areaNames;
    
    WaypointDatabase() {
        // Initialize with known intermediate areas between cities
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Sidoarjo"] = {"Waru", "Gedangan"};
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Gresik"] = {"Tandes", "Margomulyo", "Benowo"};
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Malang"] = {"Waru", "Sidoarjo", "Porong", "Pandaan", "Lawang"};
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Mojokerto"] = {"Sepanjang", "Krian", "Mojosari"};
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Lamongan"] = {"Gresik", "Cerme", "Duduk Sampeyan"};
        areaNames["Surabaya"]["Probolinggo"] = {"Sidoarjo", "Pasuruan", "Kraksaan"};
        
        areaNames["Jakarta"]["Bogor"] = {"Depok", "Citayam", "Cibinong"};
        areaNames["Jakarta"]["Bekasi"] = {"Cakung", "Tambun", "Cikarang"};
        areaNames["Jakarta"]["Tangerang"] = {"Kalideres", "Batu Ceper", "Tanah Tinggi"};
        areaNames["Jakarta"]["Bandung"] = {"Bekasi", "Cikampek", "Purwakarta", "Padalarang"};
        
        areaNames["Yogyakarta"]["Solo"] = {"Klaten", "Prambanan", "Kartasura"};
        areaNames["Yogyakarta"]["Semarang"] = {"Magelang", "Secang", "Ambarawa", "Ungaran"};
        
        areaNames["Bandung"]["Cimahi"] = {"Pasteur", "Cihampelas", "Lembang"};
        areaNames["Bandung"]["Jakarta"] = {"Padalarang", "Purwakarta", "Cikampek", "Bekasi"};
    }
    
    string getWaypointName(const string& startCity, const string& endCity, int waypointIndex) {
        // First check direct route
        auto it1 = areaNames.find(startCity);
        if (it1 != areaNames.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(endCity);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                const auto& areas = it2->second;
                if (waypointIndex < areas.size()) {
                    return areas[waypointIndex];
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Then check reverse route
        it1 = areaNames.find(endCity);
        if (it1 != areaNames.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(startCity);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                const auto& areas = it2->second;
                // For reverse route, count from the end
                int reversedIndex = areas.size() - 1 - waypointIndex;
                if (reversedIndex >= 0 && reversedIndex < areas.size()) {
                    return areas[reversedIndex];
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Fallback to generic name
        return startCity + " to " + endCity + " (via Area " + to_string(waypointIndex + 1) + ")";
    }
};

// Create a global waypoint database instance
WaypointDatabase waypointDB;

// Enhanced Road Database for detailed road names
struct RoadDatabase {
    // Maps start city -> end city -> list of roads in order
    unordered_map<string, unordered_map<string, vector<string>>> detailedRoads;
    
    RoadDatabase() {
        // Surabaya routes
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Gresik"] = {
            "Jalan Tandes", "Jalan Margomulyo", "Jalan Tambak Osowilangun", 
            "Jalan Gresik", "Jalan KH. Abdul Karim"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Sidoarjo"] = {
            "Jalan Ahmad Yani", "Jalan Jenggolo", "Jalan Waru", 
            "Jalan Gedangan", "Jalan Diponegoro"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Malang"] = {
            "Jalan Ahmad Yani", "Tol Waru-Sidoarjo", "Tol Sidoarjo-Porong", 
            "Tol Porong-Pandaan", "Tol Pandaan-Malang", "Jalan Raya Malang"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Mojokerto"] = {
            "Jalan Raya Mastrip", "Tol Surabaya-Mojokerto", 
            "Jalan Jayanegara", "Jalan Pemuda"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Probolinggo"] = {
            "Jalan Ahmad Yani", "Tol Waru-Sidoarjo", "Tol Porong-Pandaan", 
            "Jalan Raya Pasuruan", "Jalan Raya Probolinggo"
        };
        
        // Jakarta routes
        detailedRoads["Jakarta"]["Bogor"] = {
            "Jalan TB Simatupang", "Jalan Raya Pasar Minggu", "Tol Jagorawi", 
            "Jalan Pajajaran", "Jalan Raya Bogor"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Jakarta"]["Bandung"] = {
            "Jalan Gatot Subroto", "Tol Jakarta-Cikampek", "Tol Cipularang", 
            "Tol Padalarang-Cileunyi", "Jalan Pasteur", "Jalan Asia Afrika"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Jakarta"]["Bekasi"] = {
            "Jalan Kalimalang", "Jalan Raya Bekasi", "Jalan Ahmad Yani Bekasi"
        };
        
        // Bandung routes
        detailedRoads["Bandung"]["Cimahi"] = {
            "Jalan Sukajadi", "Jalan Dr. Djunjunan", "Jalan Pasteur", 
            "Jalan Cihampelas", "Jalan Cimahi"
        };
        
        // Yogyakarta routes
        detailedRoads["Yogyakarta"]["Solo"] = {
            "Jalan Solo", "Jalan Ring Road Timur", "Jalan Prambanan", 
            "Jalan Yogya-Klaten", "Jalan Slamet Riyadi"
        };
        
        // Add non-toll alternatives
        detailedRoads["Surabaya"]["Malang-NoToll"] = {
            "Jalan Ahmad Yani", "Jalan Trosobo", "Jalan Raya Sidoarjo", 
            "Jalan Raya Porong", "Jalan Raya Gempol", "Jalan Raya Bangil", 
            "Jalan Raya Lawang", "Jalan Raya Singosari", "Jalan Raya Malang"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Jakarta"]["Bandung-NoToll"] = {
            "Jalan Raya Bogor", "Jalan Raya Puncak", "Jalan Raya Cianjur", 
            "Jalan Raya Padalarang", "Jalan Raya Cimahi", "Jalan Pasteur"
        };
        
        // Scenic routes
        detailedRoads["Jakarta"]["Bandung-Scenic"] = {
            "Jalan Raya Puncak", "Panorama Puncak", "Kebun Teh Puncak", 
            "Jalan Wisata Cianjur", "Jalur Pemandangan Lembang", "Jalan Setiabudhi"
        };
        
        detailedRoads["Yogyakarta"]["Solo-Scenic"] = {
            "Jalan Kaliurang", "Jalur Gunung Merapi", "Panorama Selo", 
            "Jalur Wisata Tawangmangu", "Jalan Karanganyar"
        };
    }
    
    vector<string> getRoadNames(const string& startCity, const string& endCity, RouteType routeType) {
        string routeKey = endCity;
        
        // Modify key for special route types
        if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
            routeKey = endCity + "-NoToll";
            // If no specific no-toll route, fall back to regular route
            if (detailedRoads[startCity].find(routeKey) == detailedRoads[startCity].end()) {
                routeKey = endCity;
            }
        } else if (routeType == SCENIC) {
            routeKey = endCity + "-Scenic";
            // If no specific scenic route, fall back to regular route
            if (detailedRoads[startCity].find(routeKey) == detailedRoads[startCity].end()) {
                routeKey = endCity;
            }
        }
        
        // Check direct route
        auto it1 = detailedRoads.find(startCity);
        if (it1 != detailedRoads.end()) {
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(routeKey);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                // Filter out toll roads if avoiding tolls and using the regular route
                if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS && routeKey == endCity) {
                    vector<string> noTollRoads;
                    for (const auto& road : it2->second) {
                        if (road.find("Tol") == string::npos) {
                            noTollRoads.push_back(road);
                        } else {
                            // Add alternative road name
                            noTollRoads.push_back("Jalan Alternatif " + road.substr(4));
                        }
                    }
                    return noTollRoads;
                }
                return it2->second;
            }
        }
        
        // Try reverse direction
        it1 = detailedRoads.find(endCity);
        if (it1 != detailedRoads.end()) {
            string reverseRouteKey = startCity;
            if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS) {
                reverseRouteKey = startCity + "-NoToll";
                if (it1->second.find(reverseRouteKey) == it1->second.end()) {
                    reverseRouteKey = startCity;
                }
            } else if (routeType == SCENIC) {
                reverseRouteKey = startCity + "-Scenic";
                if (it1->second.find(reverseRouteKey) == it1->second.end()) {
                    reverseRouteKey = startCity;
                }
            }
            
            auto it2 = it1->second.find(reverseRouteKey);
            if (it2 != it1->second.end()) {
                vector<string> reversedRoads = it2->second;
                reverse(reversedRoads.begin(), reversedRoads.end());
                
                // Filter out toll roads if avoiding tolls
                if (routeType == AVOID_TOLLS && reverseRouteKey == startCity) {
                    vector<string> noTollRoads;
                    for (const auto& road : reversedRoads) {
                        if (road.find("Tol") == string::npos) {
                            noTollRoads.push_back(road);
                        } else {
                            // Add alternative road name
                            noTollRoads.push_back("Jalan Alternatif " + road.substr(4));
                        }
                    }
                    return noTollRoads;
                }
                return reversedRoads;
            }
        }
        
        // Fallback for unknown routes - generate some plausible road names
        vector<string> fallbackRoads;
        fallbackRoads.push_back("Jalan Raya " + startCity);
        fallbackRoads.push_back("Jalan Penghubung " + startCity + "-" + endCity);
        fallbackRoads.push_back("Jalan Utama " + endCity);
        return fallbackRoads;
    }
};

// Create a global road database instance
RoadDatabase roadDB;
